It reverts to its true form if it dies., While in mist form, the vampire can't take any actions, speak, or manipulate objects. In addition, if air can pass through a space, the mist can do so without squeezing, and it can't pass through water. If it can't transform, it is destroyed., While it has 0 hit points in mist form, it can't revert to its vampire form, and it must reach its resting place within 2 hours or be destroyed. Once in its resting place, it reverts to its vampire form. It is then <strong>paralyzed</strong> until it regains at least 1 hit point. After spending 1 hour in its resting place with 0 hit points, it regains 1 hit point.</li><li><strong>Regeneration:</strong> The vampire regains 20 hit points at the start of its turn if it has at least 1 hit point and isn't in sunlight or running water. If the vampire takes radiant damage or damage from holy water, this trait doesn't function at the start of the vampire's next turn.</li><li><strong>Spider Climb:</strong> The vampire can climb difficult surfaces, including upside down on ceilings, without needing to make an ability check.</li><li><strong>Vampire Weaknesses:</strong> The vampire has the following flaws:, TAG:i The vampire can't enter a residence without an invitation from one of the occupants., TAG:i The vampire takes 20 acid damage if it ends its turn in running water., TAG:i If a piercing weapon made of wood is driven into the vampire's heart while the vampire is <strong>incapacitated</strong> in its resting place, the vampire is <strong>paralyzed</strong> until the stake is removed., TAG:i The vampire takes 20 radiant damage when it starts its turn in sunlight. While in sunlight, it has disadvantage on attack rolls and ability checks.</li> </ul></div>   <hr/> <h6>Actions</h6> <div><ul> <li><strong>Multiattack (Vampire Form Only):</strong> The vampire makes two attacks, only one of which can be a bite attack.</li><li><strong>Unarmed Strike (Vampire Form Only):</strong> <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='1d20+9' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('1d20+9');"><strong><strong>+9</strong></strong></a> to hit, reach 5 ft., one creature. If the curse reduces the target's hit point maximum to 0, the target dies, and its body turns to dust. The curse lasts until removed by the TAG:spell spell or other magic.</li><li><strong>Dreadful Glare:</strong> The mummy targets one creature it can see within 60 feet of it. If the target can see the mummy, it must succeed on a <strong>DC11</strong> Wisdom saving throw against this magic or become <strong>frightened</strong> until the end of the mummy's next turn. If the target fails the saving throw by 5 or more, it is also <strong>paralyzed</strong> for the same duration. A target that succeeds on the saving throw is immune to the Dreadful Glare of all mummies (but not mummy lords) for the next 24 hours.</li> </ul></div>  </div> </div> </div> </div> </td> </tr>    </table>
